============================================================
-04- COMMANDS
------------------------------------------------------------

3xEarth
-------
3 times, use a random earth-elemental skill.

  (3/8 chance each)  Magnitude8
  (2/8 chance each)  Quake
  (1/8 chance each)  LifeShaver, Slide, Terrato

Bolt2
-------
Use the skill 'Bolt 2'

CleanSw
-------
Use the skill 'CleanSweep'

ConMega
-------
Use the combo Condemned + Megahit.

Float
-------
Use the skill 'Float'

HeaSabr
-------
Use the combo Heal Force + Sabre Soul.

L5Doom
-------
Use the skill 'L.5 Doom'

MindWar
-------
Use the combo Mind Blast + Warp.

Rage
-------
Use the skill 'Rage'

StoLife
-------
Use the combo Stop + Life 3.

W-BlCur
-------
2 times, use the combo Blaster + Cure.
